\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00032}00032\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00033}00033\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{The\ goal\ of\ this\ script\ is\ to\ identify\ places\ in\ the\ code\ that\ *may*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00034}00034\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{be\ in\ non-\/compliance\ with\ google\ style.\ \ It\ does\ not\ attempt\ to\ fix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00035}00035\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{up\ these\ problems\ -\/-\/\ the\ point\ is\ to\ educate.\ \ It\ does\ also\ not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00036}00036\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{attempt\ to\ find\ all\ problems,\ or\ to\ ensure\ that\ everything\ it\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00037}00037\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{find\ is\ legitimately\ a\ problem.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00038}00038\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00039}00039\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{In\ particular,\ we\ can\ get\ very\ confused\ by\ /*\ and\ //\ inside\ strings!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00040}00040\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{We\ do\ a\ small\ hack,\ which\ is\ to\ ignore\ //'s\ with\ "{}'s\ after\ them\ on\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{cpplint_8py_source_l00041}00041\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{same\ line,\ but\ it\ is\ far\ from\ perfect\ (in\ either\ direction).}}
